A NATIONAL LEVEL JAIHIND INNOFEST-2K22 shall be conducted by Jaihind College of Engineering, Kuran.
JAIHIND INNOFEST-2K22 aims at identification of ideas that have the capability to convert into an enterprise from youth who are studying in the colleges.
*Themes*:
1. SMART Agriculture
2. Healthcare
3. IoT 
4. Robotic in Automation
5. Electric Mobility
6. SMART 
7. E-waste collection and disposal             
8. Remedies to tackle air pollution                                                                       
9. Innovation solution for recycling at residential and commercial unit level
*Eligibility*:
1. JAIHIND INNOFEST-2K22 is a team based competition open to Engineering and Polytechnic college students.
2. Eligible students can participate only in teams of 1 to 4 members.
3. The only way to participate in JAIHIND INNOFEST-2K22 is by submitting an idea at the online link https://forms.gle/wVxRm6RqFpJWQzSv6.
4. The idea submission form will close at the Noon of 11th October 2022. 
   Upon closure, no entry for JAIHIND INNOFEST-2K22 shall be considered for evaluation.
5. Participation in, JAIHIND INNOFEST-2K22 is FREE. 
6. The presentation by the team shall be as per given template.
7. On 13th October 2022, all submitted ideas shall be presented and evaluated by our expert panel.

*Prizes*: 
Winner of JAIHIND INNOFEST-2K22 shall be awarded with First Prize 5000/-, second Prize 3000/- and third 2000/-with certificates


*Certification of Participation*: 

All participation shall get a Certificate of Participation to all teams at College level. 

*Selection Criteria*:
1. Problem statement given by the team should be innovative.
2. Solution provided by the teams should be practical and implementable.
3. Startup idea should have the potential to scale-up and should not be easily replicable.
4. Team members should be committed to pursue the idea for commercialization.

11/24/22, 23:08 - Prof. Dr Uday Patka(HOD): The grand inaugration of UNESCO INDIA-AFRICA Hackathon 2022 was done by Hon'ble Chief Minister Adityanath Yogi. 
Our theme was drinking water and sanitation and in this problem statement was Aquifer Mapping and Management of Ground Water Resources. 
36 hours of hackathon it was, at night while hackathon was going on our Chief Executive Officer (Abhay Jhere) came, met us and took a picture with us. 
The journey of the Hackathon was amazing I enjoyed a lot and learnt new things. It was a great experience with the African students. Some of the African students were unable to understand English, we guys were facing difficulty in communicating with them so, we used Google Translator for communication. But still the African students gave their best ЁЯСН and they all are happy because they all have got chance to visit India. 
The Inaugration of this hackathon was amazing. All participating students represented their country by wearing their traditional dresses. 
The entire journey of this International Hackathon was overwhelming.

*Presentation Competition*

*тАЬIdeaIn10 (2022)-Pune RegionтАЭ*
 
 
We are happy to inform you that the IET Pune LNтАЩs presentation competition тАЬIdeaIn10 (2022) - Pune RegionтАЭ  will be organized at MIT-WPU Campus, Kothrud, Pune. The тАЬIdeaIn10 (2022) - Pune RegionтАЭ competition is open for the students of Engineering and Technology, graduates and young professionals from Pune Region, aged 18 тАУ 30 years. This competition will provide a platform to young minds to explore and showcase their presentation and technical skills. 

*Details for participation in тАЬIdeaIn10 (2022) - Pune RegionтАЭ competition*
*Date of Competition*: 10th December 2022
*Time*: 10:00 am onwards
*Venue*: Second Floor, Dhruv Building, Faculty of Engineering & Technology, MIT WPU Campus, Kothrud, Pune 

*Registration Link*: https://forms.gle/ZXxJNphuL54uUEMt7 

*Eligibility Criteria: Engineering students, recent graduates, apprentices and young professionals from Pune region, aged 18 to 30 years can participate.

*Note* 
*Registration is compulsory
*Last date of Registration is 5th December 2022.


*Briefing notes for competitors*
This Competition is organized by IET Pune Local Network 
Present the technical topic (subject related to Engineering and Technology) for 10 mins
Presentation on Final year project having societal or industry relevance is also acceptable
Competitors should provide a brief synopsis of their presentation (100-200 words) as a hard copy during presentation
Competitors should carry their presentation in Pen drive, and have to upload on the system at the venue before the session starts
*The prizes are: Certificate and prize money to winner and Runner up of Rs. 14000/- and Rs. 9000/- respectively and participation certificate to all other participants*

12/16/22, 16:14 - Prof. Dr Uday Patka(HOD): Greetings of the day..

We hope this email finds you in the best of spirits in these tough times.

We are happy to inform you that the Government of India has taken up various initiatives for the upliftment of Scheduled Castes (SCs), Scheduled Tribes (STs), Women and Economically Weaker Section (EWS) in the country. This includes scholarships, Free Coaching, Economic empowerment schemes and related activities. As the efforts in this direction is significant for upliftment of various sections of the society, there is a need to provide adequate opportunity for candidates to gain expertise and skills in Information Technology, Electronics and related domains which are expected to be leveraged in near future.

Considering these aspects Work Based Learning (WBL) programme in Niche/Emerging Technologies is a unique initiative to provide employability skills to the individuals of SC, ST, Women and EWS.

The Key Features of the WBL:

This programme will provide an opportunity to selected SC/ST/EWS/Women candidates to acquire Technical Knowledge Expansion; Real-time Working Skills; Technology Use; Problem Solving Skills; Reasoning; Ideation; Analytical Thinking; Interpersonal Skills, etc. in a professional work environment. This programme would aim to achieve the following: 

It facilitates SC/ ST/ EWS/ Women candidates for transition from college environment to the corporate world, and thereby provides them with a real-time exposure on niche technological project/ activity in organizations under MeitY.
The Programme provides direct practical experience and exposure to Fresh Graduates Engineers on Niche Technologies thereby reducing the тАЬdeployable timeтАЭ for both the candidate, as well as the prospective employer.
It helps candidates attain stability between theoretical studies and realistic job exposure through hand-on expertise in Design/Developmental Skills, Requirement Analysis, Testing skills, Exposure to Standardization/QA etc.
Helps in enhancing professional skills among the candidates in various areas such as problem-solving abilities; communication skills; presentation skills, confidence enhancement, individual grooming, enterprise etiquettes, etc.
Perks for the candidates

* Completion Certificate
* Stipend- INR 10,000 per month
* Placement Assistance

Period of Programme- 6 Months (Next batch Commencing on- Jan/Feb 2023)

Some of the Key technologies that can be leveraged under the programme are:

Artificial Intelligence (AI) and Machine Learning
Robotic Process Automation (RPA)
Quantum Computing тАв Augmented Reality & Virtual Reality (AR/VR)
Block chain
Wireless Networks (5G, Wi-Fi 6 etc.)
Smart Mobility (Including Vehicular and Drone Technology)
Internet of Things (IOT)
Cyber Security and Cyber Forensics
Big Data Analytics
Digital Preservation
Cloud Computing
3D Printing
Flexible Electronics
Emerging Memory/ Storage Technologies
Machine vision (MV)
CPU Design
Area of work / activities in the organization can include specific / targeted project work, capability building initiatives, design-based activities, developmental activities, research-based activities, etc.

Individual will get the opportunity to work on Live Projects and Technologies.

WBL is facilitated through Seven (7) Organizations of MeitY i.e. CERT-IN, C-DAC, NIELIT, STQC, CMET, ERNET and SAMEER constituting of total 81 Centers or Units.

These opportunities are available on AICTE internship portal.

Internship Opportunities can be found here:
https://internship.aicte-india.org/ernet.php

It is requested to share this information among your student network and ask them to register on the portal and avail the benefits.

We hope that our internship portal, which is entirely free of cost, will be helpful to your students in adapting to a transparent internship process and abundant access to real, credible and the most genuine opportunities.

For any clarifications, feel free to contact us.

With Regards,
Dr. Buddha Chandrasekhar,

Theme for the 8th edition of IISF is Marching Towards Amrit Kaal with Science, Technology and Innovation.
